\end{DoxyCode}
This macro will allocate memory for an array and assign that memory to the array pointer variable in a struct. The macro will also assign the number of allocated indices to allocated\+\_\+length and assign active\+\_\+length a size of 0. This function requires the input of a struct instantiated with the VECTOR\+\_\+\+STRUCT method.

/param vec A vector instantiated with the VECTOR\+\_\+\+STRUCT macro. /length The length of the array as a size\+\_\+t variable

\index{vector.h@{vector.h}!VECTOR\_STRUCT@{VECTOR\_STRUCT}}
\index{VECTOR\_STRUCT@{VECTOR\_STRUCT}!vector.h@{vector.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{VECTOR\_STRUCT}{VECTOR\_STRUCT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define VECTOR\+\_\+\+STRUCT(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{type,  }\item[{}]{dtype }\end{DoxyParamCaption})~ typedef struct \{type $\ast$array; size\+\_\+t allocated\+\_\+length; size\+\_\+t active\+\_\+length; \mbox{\hyperlink{vector_8h_ad756268621f03e4812b68792b291fff5}{mem\+\_\+type}} dat\+\_\+type; \} dtype}

This macro will produce a struct that is specifically designed to track all attributes necessary for the maintenance of a dynamically, or statically allocated array. The macro has an attribute to a pointer for the array, allocated\+\_\+length, active\+\_\+length, and mem\+\_\+type.

/param type The data type that will be assigned to the array pointer /param dtype The name to be given to the typedef for the struct

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pop\_ushort\_vector\_index()}{pop\_ushort\_vector\_index()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int pop\+\_\+ushort\+\_\+vector\+\_\+index (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{UShort $\ast$}]{vec,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{index }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This function will pop a value from an UShort struct container as a user defined index. This function runs fastest, when the index is the last populated index.

/param vec An struct container of type UShort /param index The index from which data is to be popped.

This function will sort a vector data structure of type UShort in forward or reverse order

/param vec A vector data structure of type UShort /param low The lowest indice for partitioning, recommended to be 0 /param high The highest indice for sorting, recommended to be the last index in the data structure /param order FORWARD for a forward sort, REVERSE for a reverse sort

\DoxyCodeLine{03454     \textcolor{comment}{// To find integral part of square}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03455     \textcolor{comment}{// root of number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03456     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (start <= end) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03457         \textcolor{comment}{// Find mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03458         mid = (start + end) / 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03459         \textcolor{comment}{// If number is perfect square}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03460         \textcolor{comment}{// then break}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03461         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (mid * mid == number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03462             ans = mid;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03463             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{03464         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03465         \textcolor{comment}{// Increment start if integral}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03466         \textcolor{comment}{// part lies on right side}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03467         \textcolor{comment}{// of the mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03468         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (mid * mid < number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03469           \textcolor{comment}{//first start value should be added to answer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03470             ans=start;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03471           \textcolor{comment}{//then start should be changed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03472             start = mid + 1.f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03473         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03474         \textcolor{comment}{// Decrement end if integral part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03475         \textcolor{comment}{// lies on the left side of the mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03476         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03477             end = mid -\/ 1.f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03478         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03479     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03480     \textcolor{comment}{// To find the fractional part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03481     \textcolor{comment}{// of square root upto 5 decimal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03482     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} increment = 0.1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03483     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < 5; i++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03484         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (ans * ans <= number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03485             ans += increment;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03486         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03487         \textcolor{comment}{// Loop terminates,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03488         \textcolor{comment}{// when ans * ans > number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03489         ans = ans -\/ increment;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03490         increment = increment / 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03491     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03492     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ans;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03493 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03339     \textcolor{comment}{// root of number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03340     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (start <= end) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03341         \textcolor{comment}{// Find mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03342         mid = (start + end) / 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03343         \textcolor{comment}{// If number is perfect square}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03344         \textcolor{comment}{// then break}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03345         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (mid * mid == number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03346             ans = mid;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03347             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{03348         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03349         \textcolor{comment}{// Increment start if integral}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03350         \textcolor{comment}{// part lies on right side}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03351         \textcolor{comment}{// of the mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03352         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (mid * mid < number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03353           \textcolor{comment}{//first start value should be added to answer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03354             ans=start;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03355           \textcolor{comment}{//then start should be changed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03356             start = mid + 1.f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03357         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03358         \textcolor{comment}{// Decrement end if integral part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03359         \textcolor{comment}{// lies on the left side of the mid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03360         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03361             end = mid -\/ 1.f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03362         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03363     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03364     \textcolor{comment}{// To find the fractional part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03365     \textcolor{comment}{// of square root upto 5 decimal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03366     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} increment = 0.1f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03367     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < 5; i++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03368         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (ans * ans <= number) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{03369             ans += increment;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03370         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03371         \textcolor{comment}{// Loop terminates,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03372         \textcolor{comment}{// when ans * ans > number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03373         ans = ans -\/ increment;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03374         increment = increment / 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03375     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03376     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ans;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03377 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03634         \textcolor{comment}{// then break}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03636             ans = mid;}

\DoxyCodeLine{03653     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03664         increment = increment / 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{03665     \}}
